<div class="col-a">
<div id="page-1135" class="elements-box post-1135 page type-page status-publish hentry">
<h5><span style="color: #339966;">အရွင္ဘဒၵႏ ၱသုနႏၵ ေဟာၾကားေတာ္မူေသာ တရားေတာ္မ်ား စုစည္းမွု (MP3)</span></h5>
<h5><span style="color: #339966;"><a href="https://www.thitsarparamisociety.com/u-thu-nanda-mp4/" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">အရွင္ဘဒၵႏ ၱသုနႏၵ ေဟာၾကားေတာ္မူေသာ တရားေတာ္မ်ား စုစည္းမွု (MP4) Click Here</span></a><br>
</span></h5>
<h3></h3>
<h5><strong><span style="color: #339966;">၂၀၁၆ ၊ စက္တင္ဘာလ ၁၀.၀၉.၂၀၁၅ မွ ၁၂.၀၉.၁၆ ထိ စကၤာပူ ႏိုင္ငံ သစၥာပါရမီေက်ာင္း (၃၀၈) ႀကိမ္ေျမာက္ </span></strong></h5>
<h5><strong><span style="color: #339966;">၃ ရက္တာ အခ်ိန္ျပည့္ တရား စခန္း တြင္ ေဟာၾကားအပ္ေသာ တရားေတာ္ မ်ား</span></strong></h5>
<p><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/U%20Thu%20Nan%20Da%20%20(Mogok)/3DAYSINGAPORE2016/1st7pm100916.mp3"><span style="color: #ff9900;"> ေသနည္းသံုးဖ်ာခြဲသိပါ (၁) (၁၀.၉.၁၆) ညခ်မ္းတရားေတာ္</span></a></p>
<p><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/U%20Thu%20Nan%20Da%20%20(Mogok)/3DAYSINGAPORE2016/2ND7PM110916.mp3"><span style="color: #ff9900;"> ေသနည္းသံုးဖ်ာခြဲသိပါ (၂) (၁၁.၉.၁၆) ညခ်မ္းတရားေတာ္</span></a></p>
<p><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/U%20Thu%20Nan%20Da%20%20(Mogok)/3DAYSINGAPORE2016/2nd4pm110916.mp3"><span style="color: #ff9900;"> ေဝသနာႏုပႆနာရွဳ ပြားနည္း (၁၁.၉.၁၆) ညေန ပိုင္း </span></a></p>
<p><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/U%20Thu%20Nan%20Da%20%20(Mogok)/3DAYSINGAPORE2016/3rd7pm120916.mp3"><span style="color: #ff9900;"> ကံႀကီးထိုက္မွာေၾကာက္စရာ (၁၂.၉.၁၆) ညခ်မ္းတရားေတာ္ </span></a></p>
<p><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/U%20Thu%20Nan%20Da%20%20(Mogok)/3DAYSINGAPORE2016/3rd4pm120916.mp3"><span style="color: #ff9900;"> လကၡဏ ဉာဏ္ျမင္နိဗၺာန္ဝင္ (၁၂.၉.၁၆) ညေနပိုင္း</span></a></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h5><strong><span style="color: #339966;">၂၀၁၅ ၊ ၾသဂုတ္လ ၇.၀၈.၂၀၁၅ မွ ၁၀.၀၈.၂၀၁၅ ထိ စကၤာပူ ႏိုင္ငံ သစၥာပါရမီေက်ာင္း (၂၅၃) ႀကိမ္ေျမာက္ </span></strong></h5>
<h5><strong><span style="color: #339966;">၄ ရက္တာ အခ်ိန္ျပည့္ တရား စခန္း တြင္ ေဟာၾကားအပ္ေသာ တရားေတာ္ မ်ား</span></strong></h5>
<p><br style="color: #222222;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/U%20Thu%20Nan%20Da%20%20(Mogok)/Thitsarparami/Alotepay.MP3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၀၁။ ရွစ္ပါး သီလေပး ႏွင့္ အလုပ္ေပးတရားေတာ္</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/U%20Thu%20Nan%20Da%20%20(Mogok)/Thitsarparami/Day-1(1).MP3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၀၂။ (၇.၀၈.၁၅) ေန႔လည္ခင္း ေဟာ ၾကားအပ္ေသာ ခႏၵာဉာဏ္ေရာက္ ဒိ႒ိေပ်ာက္ ပဋိစၥသမုပၸဒ္သင္တန္းတရားေတာ္</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/U%20Thu%20Nan%20Da%20%20(Mogok)/Thitsarparami/Day-1(2).MP3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၀၃။ (၇.၀၈.၂၀၁၅) ညေနခင္း ေဟာၾကားအပ္ေသာ ပုဂၢိဳလ္ ေလးမ်ိဳး က်င့္စဥ္ေလးျဖာတရားေတာ္</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/U%20Thu%20Nan%20Da%20%20(Mogok)/Thitsarparami/Day-2-1.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၀၄။ (၈.၀၈.၂၀၁၅) ေန႔လည္ခင္း ေဟာၾကားအပ္ေသာ ခႏၲာဉာဏ္ေရာက္ ဒိ႒ိေပ်ာက္ ပဋိစၥသမုပၸာဒ္သင္တန္းတရားေတာ္</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/U%20Thu%20Nan%20Da%20%20(Mogok)/Thitsarparami/Day-2(2).MP3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၀၅။ (၈.၀၈.၂၀၁၅) ညေနခင္း ေဟာၾကားအပ္ေသာ အေျခခံဝိပႆနာရႈပြားနည္းတရားေတာ္</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/U%20Thu%20Nan%20Da%20%20(Mogok)/Thitsarparami/Day-3-1.MP3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၀၆။ (၉.၀၈.၂၀၁၅) ေန႔လည္ခင္း ေဟာၾကားအပ္ေသာ ခႏၲာဉာဏ္ေရာက္ ဒိ႒ိေပ်ာက္ ပဋိစၥသမုပၸာဒ္သင္တန္းတရားေတာ္</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/U%20Thu%20Nan%20Da%20%20(Mogok)/Thitsarparami/Day-3-2.MP3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၀၇။ (၉.၀၈.၂၀၁၅) ညေနခင္း ေဟာၾကားအပ္ေသာ အေျခခံ ဝိပႆနာ ရႈပြားနည္း အလုပ္သင္တရားေတာ္</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/U%20Thu%20Nan%20Da%20%20(Mogok)/Thitsarparami/Day-4-1.MP3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၀၈။ (၁၀.၀၈.၂၀၁၅) ေန႔လည္ခင္း ေဟာၾကားအပ္ေသာ ခႏၲာဉာဏ္ေရာက္ ဒိ႒ိေပ်ာက္ ပဋိစၥသမုပၸာဒ္သင္တန္းတရားေတာ္</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/U%20Thu%20Nan%20Da%20%20(Mogok)/Thitsarparami/Day-4-2.MP3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၀၉။ (၁၀.၀၈.၂၀၁၅) ညေနခင္း ေဟာၾကားအပ္ေသာ ေလာကီမဂ္ ႏွင့္ ေလာကုတၱရာမဂ္ ထူးျခားပံု အလုပ္သင္တရားေတာ္</span></a></span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h5><span style="color: #339966;">အရွင္ဘဒၵႏ ၱသုနႏၵ ေဟာၾကားေတာ္မူေသာ တရားေတာ္မ်ား စုစည္းမွု (၅၀၀ ပုဒ္)</span></h5>

<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/U%20Thu%20Nan%20Da%20%20%28Mogok%29/500/504%20-%20APhone%285%29Thawe.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၀၀၄။ အဖံုးငါးသြယ္ ဖယ္ရႈဖြယ္ အလုပ္ေပး</span></a></span></p>

<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/U%20Thu%20Nan%20Da%20%20%28Mogok%29/500/507%20-%2022.08.2004.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၀၀၇။ ၂၂-၀၈-၂၀၀၄ ကုသိုလ္စစ္မွ စိတ္ခ်ရ (၂)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/U%20Thu%20Nan%20Da%20%20%28Mogok%29/500/508%20-%2023.08.2004.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၀၀၈။ ၂၃-၀၈-၂၀၀၄ ျမဳပ္ေမ်ာ ေရွာင္ၾကဥ္ဆန္လမ္းယဥ္(၁)</span></a></span></p>

<div id="text-17" class="widget widget_text"><h3 class="widget-title">Feed Back</h3> <div class="textwidget"><p align="justify">ဓမၼမိတ္ေဆြ အေပါင္းတို ့ မိမိတုိ ့၏ တရားစခန္း အခက္အခဲမ်ား၊ နာၾကား အၾကံျပဳ လိုေသာ တရားဓမၼမ်ား ၊ ေမးျမန္းလိုေသာ ဓမၼေမးခြန္းမ်ား ၊ website ၾကည့္ရွုနာၾကားရာ ၌ အခက္အခဲမ်ား ျဖစ္ေပၚပါက ေအာက္ပါ Form တြင္ ျဖည့္စြက္၍ ေပးပို႔ အႀကံျပဳၾကပါရန္ ေမတၱာရပ္ခံအပ္ပါသည္။</p>

<script type="text/javascript">
		jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
			
		jQuery("#preloader-rmhsjd").fadeOut(1500, function () {
			jQuery("#ecf-form-rmhsjd").fadeIn(300);
			});
			
			$( '.ladda-button' ).ladda( 'bind' );

			$(function() {
				
						
				// Validation
				$("#form-rmhsjd").validate(
				{					
					// Rules for form validation
					rules:
					{
					name0:{required: true},email1:{required: true,email: true},message2:{required: true,minlength: 10},
							
									
					},
										
					// Messages for form validation
					messages:
					{
					name0:{required: "This field is required"},email1:{required: "This field is required"},message2:{required: "This field is required"}					},					
					// Do not change code below
					errorPlacement: function(error, element) {
						error.insertAfter(element.parent());
						},
						
					submitHandler: function (form) {
										 ecf_onsubmit(jQuery('.form-rmhsjd'));
						 
						 						 
						 },
						 
					invalidHandler: function (form) {	
					  	$.ladda( 'stopAll' );
					 	},
						 
					onkeyup: false,
					onfocusout: false,
					onclick: false
					
				});
			});	
			
			
			/* Form Submit ( Ajax ) */
			function ecf_onsubmit(form){	

				if(form.attr('action')=='#'){
					
					data = {};
					eldat = [];
					data['action'] = 'ecf_deliver_mail';
					data['formid'] = '12786';
					data['security'] = '00534cad96';
		
		
						
					jQuery('input, textarea', form).each(function(key){
						
						items = {};
						
						if (typeof $(this).data('type') === 'undefined') { return true; }
						

						
						items['type'] = $(this).data('type');
						items['label'] = $(this).data('label');
						items['value'] = this.value;
						items['name'] = this.name;

						eldat.push(items);
							
						}); // END  form).each(function(key){
							

													

						data['allelmnt'] = JSON.stringify(eldat);

						submitForm();
				
					return false;
					
				} // End if(form.attr('action')=='#'){
				
			} // End ecf_onsubmit 
			
			// Start submitForm		
			  function submitForm() {
				  
				jQuery.ajax({
					url: 'https://www.thitsarparamisociety.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', 
					type: 'POST',
					dataType: 'json',
					data: data, 
					success: function(data) {
				
						if(data.Ok==true) {
									// success
							$("#form-rmhsjd").get(0).reset();	
								
							if(data.msg == 'redirect') {
								window.location = "http://";
								} else {
									notifyme('Your Message Submitted Successfully', 'n', 'success', 'left middle');
									}
		
							}
							else {
								$("#form-rmhsjd").get(0).reset();
								notifyme(data.msg, 'n', 'error', 'left middle');
								}
								
							$.ladda( 'stopAll' );	
									
							}
						});
						
										
					} // End submitForm
	
					
			// Notify	
			  function notifyme(msg, b, typ, pos) {
				  if (b == 'n') {
					  b = 'cf-submittedrmhsjd';
				  } else {
					 b = 'atcrmhsjd';
				  }
				  
				  $("#"+b).gnotify(msg,{
					  style: "nbootstrap",
					  elementPosition: pos,
					  className: typ
					  });
					  
					  msg = null;
					  typ = null;
					  
					}

		});		
		</script>

</fieldset>

	}

		w = settings.contentWidth;

		w = data.model.width;
	}

		h = Math.ceil( ( data.model.height * w ) / data.model.width );
	} else {
		h = data.model.height;
 	}
